Create a platform file prompt dialog to choose a directory path for opening/saving a directory. N\+O\+TE\+: this method will block the main thread 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dir} & Non const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_w_d_l___string}{W\+D\+L\+\_\+\+String}} reference specifying the directory path. Set this prior to calling the method for save dialogs, to provide a default path. For load dialogs, on successful selection of a directory this will get set to the full path. \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void I\+Graphics\+::\+Prompt\+For\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_w_d_l___string}{W\+D\+L\+\_\+\+String}} \&}]{file\+Name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_w_d_l___string}{W\+D\+L\+\_\+\+String}} \&}]{path,  }\item[{E\+File\+Action}]{action = {\ttfamily EFileAction\+:\+:Open},  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{ext = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\char`\"{}},  }\item[{I\+File\+Dialog\+Completion\+Handler\+Func}]{completion\+Handler = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Create a platform file prompt dialog to choose a path for opening/saving a single file. N\+O\+TE\+: this method will block the main thread on mac\+OS, unless you speficy the completion\+Hander, which will be called asynchronously when the dialog button is pressed. On i\+OS, you must supply a completion\+Hander. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Name} & Non const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_w_d_l___string}{W\+D\+L\+\_\+\+String}} reference specifying the file name. Set this prior to calling the method for save dialogs, to provide a default file name. For file-\/open dialogs, on successful selection of a file this will get set to the file’s name. \\
\hline
{\em path} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_w_d_l___string}{W\+D\+L\+\_\+\+String}} reference where the path will be put on success or empty string on failure/user cancelled \\
\hline
{\em action} & Determines whether this is an file-\/open dialog or a file-\/save dialog \\
\hline
{\em ext} & A space separated C\+String list of file extensions to filter in the dialog (e.\+g. “.\+wav .aif” \\
\hline
{\em completion\+Handler} & an I\+File\+Dialog\+Completion\+Handler\+Func that will be called when a file is selected or the dialog is cancelled \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
